# Text Elements
Phase 1
[[Card Phase]] ^hCiIc7O3

User picks x Cards from predefined Deck
-> Cards can be used in Phase 2 and 3 to 
trigger diffrent effects  ^o4QyeCNI

Phase 2
[[Laning Phase]] ^16pAQP2j

User Controlls Army to follow lane.
Each lane can have different effect 
on passing units. User can use cards to 
trigger effects.
-> Build building on next lane ? 
-> Add more units?

Lane Events.
-> Upgrading 
-> Fighting
 ^BP2QejVK

Phase 3
[[Battle Phase]] ^S3iRPZV9

The Units that survived lanign phase
Fight against a other players units.
Cards can be triggered to controll 
the battlefield  ^B3Shrm1T

The 3 phases loop for 3(?) Time till just one player survives ^9ZZ4JFQp

[[Shop]] ^HZx2cZkd

In the Shop the player can purchase
different Booster packs, Skins(?).
Booster:
    - Contain 10 cards
    - With diffrent rarity 
Skins: 
    - For units
    - For lane
    - for battlefield
    - Avatar 
    - Emotes     ^7c6j2Q7B

%%
